7/10/23, 7:20 AM - Mannkumar Pandya: <!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
    <title>Bar Chart</title>
</head>
<body>
    <canvas id="myCanvas" width="500" height="500"></canvas>

    <script>
        var myCanvas = document.getElementById("myCanvas");
        var ctx = myCanvas.getContext("2d");

        var data = [100, 68, 20, 30, 100];
        var labels = ["Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May"];
        var colors = ["#49A9EA", "#36CAAB", "#34495E", "#B370CF", "#AC5353"];

        var width = 50;
        var currX = 50;
        var base = 200;

        ctx.fillStyle = "#000";
        ctx.fillText("Sales", 10, 20);

        for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
            var h = data[i];
            ctx.fillStyle = colors[i];
            ctx.fillRect(currX, base - h, width, h);
            currX += width + 20;

            ctx.fillStyle = "#000";
            ctx.fillText(labels[i], currX - width - 10, base + 20);
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

Step 1 375/26 = 14.423 ( take only decimal) 

14×26 =364 (jenthi divide karyu enathi j multiply karva nu eetle 375 ne nearest number mdse ) 

Now je number nu mod find kari rahya che e number mathi je answer madyo e minus kar devano (375 - 364 = 11) 
11 is final answer
